58:["$","p",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Symptom:"}]," When ",["$","code",null,{"children":"(p-selected)"}]," fires and you want to reject the selection (e.g., guard\nvalidation failed), setting ",["$","code",null,{"children":"$$selected: false"}]," on the item synchronously has no effect.\nThe row stays visually selected, and clicking it again fires ",["$","code",null,{"children":"(p-selected)"}]," instead of\n",["$","code",null,{"children":"(p-unselected)"}],", so the warning message fires a second time."]}]
59:["$","p",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Root cause:"}]," po-table adds the row to its internal ",["$","code",null,{"children":"selectedRows"}]," array ",["$","strong",null,{"children":"before"}],"\ndispatching the ",["$","code",null,{"children":"(p-selected)"}]," event. Any synchronous ",["$","code",null,{"children":"$$selected: false"}]," change on the\nitems signal is processed in the same change-detection cycle — but po-table's internal\nstate already has the row, so the visual state stays selected even though the data says\n",["$","code",null,{"children":"$$selected: false"}],". This desync causes a second ",["$","code",null,{"children":"(p-selected)"}]," on the next click instead\nof ",["$","code",null,{"children":"(p-unselected)"}],"."]}]
5a:["$","p",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Fix:"}]," Defer the items array replacement to ",["$","code",null,{"children":"setTimeout(0)"}],". This lets the current\nevent cycle complete, then replaces the items array in the next microtask. po-table's\n",["$","code",null,{"children":"ngOnChanges"}]," receives the new array and reinitializes its selection from ",["$","code",null,{"children":"$$selected"}],",\ncorrectly showing the row as unselected."]}]
